The easiest way to perform iterative operations"230 PRINT "is to employ FOR/NEXT loops.

"240 PRINT "     In a FOR/NEXT loop you specify the starting value"250 PRINT "of a variable, the final value of the variable, and the"260 PRINT "increment by which the variable changes in each";270 PRINT " loop.

FOR variable name = starting value TO final ";280 PRINT "value STEP increment"290 PRINT "

     The NEXT statement signifies the end of the loop and"300 PRINT "causes the program execution to branch back to the FOR";305 PRINT " statement for "310 PRINT "that variable (until the final value is reached).

   ";320 PRINT "        NEXT variable name"330 PRINT "
